#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#list){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="list"} `list`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Listing & Filtering](#listing--filtering), [`browse`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#browse), [`ls`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#ls), [`pin`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#pin), [`search`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#search), [`unpin`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#unpin)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb list [-e [<length>] | --excerpt [<length>]] [--filenames]
          [-n <limit> | --limit <limit> | --<limit>] [--no-id]
          [--no-indicator] [-p <number> | --page <number>] [--pager]
          [--paths] [-s | --sort] [-r | --reverse] [--tags]
          [-t <type> | --type <type> | --<type>]
          [<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id> | <filename> | <path> | <query>]

Options:
  -e, --excerpt [<length>]        Print an excerpt <length> lines long under
                                  each note's filename [default: 3].
  --filenames                     Print the filename for each note.
  -n, --limit <limit>, --<limit>  The maximum number of notes to list.
  --no-id                         Don't include the id in list items.
  --no-indicator                  Don't include the indicator in list items.
  -p, --page <number>             The page to view in the list paginated by
                                  a <limit> option or `nb set limit`.
  --pager                         Display output in the pager.
  --paths                         Print the full path to each item.
  -s, --sort                      Order notes by id.
  -r, --reverse                   List items in reverse order.
  --tags                          List tags in the notebook or folder.
  -t, --type <type>, --<type>     List items of <type>. <type> can be a file
                                  extension or one of the following types:
                                  archive, audio, book, bookmark, document,
                                  folder, image, note, text, video

Description:
  List notes in the current notebook.

  When <id>, <filename>, <path>, or <title> are present, the listing for the
  matching note is displayed. When no match is found, titles and filenames
  are searched for any that match <query> as a case-insensitive regular
  expression.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#listing--filtering

Indicators:
  ğŸ”‰  Audio
  ğŸ“–  Book
  ğŸ”–  Bookmark
  ğŸ”’  Encrypted
  ğŸ“‚  Folder
  ğŸŒ„  Image
  ğŸ“„  PDF, Word, or Open Office document
  ğŸ“¹  Video

See Also:
  nb help browse
  nb help ls
  nb help pin
  nb help search
  nb help unpin

Examples:
  nb list
  nb list example.md -e 10
  nb list --excerpt --no-id
  nb list --filenames --reverse
  nb list "^Example.*"
  nb list --10
  nb list --type document
  nb example:list
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#ls){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="ls"} `ls`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Listing & Filtering](#listing--filtering), [`browse`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#browse), [`list`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#list), [`pin`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#pin), [`search`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#search), [`unpin`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#unpin)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb ls [-a | --all] [-b | --browse] [-e [<length>] | --excerpt [<length>]]
        [--filenames] [-g | --gui] [-n <limit> | --limit <limit> | --<limit>]
        [--no-footer] [--no-header] [--no-id] [--no-indicator]
        [-p <number> | --page <number>] [--pager] [--paths] [-s | --sort]
        [-r | --reverse] [--tags] [-t <type> | --type <type> | --<type>]
        [<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id> | <filename> | <path> | <query>]

Options:
  -a, --all                       Print all items in the notebook. Equivalent
                                  to no limit.
  -b, --browse                    Open the specified item or current notebook
                                  with `browse` in a terminal web browser.
  -e, --excerpt [<length>]        Print an excerpt <length> lines long under
                                  each note's filename [default: 3].
  --filenames                     Print the filename for each note.
  -g, --gui                       Open the specified item or current notebook
                                  with `browse` in a GUI web browser.
  -n, --limit <limit>, --<limit>  The maximum number of listed items.
                                  [default: 15]
  --no-footer                     Print without footer.
  --no-header                     Print without header.
  --no-id                         Don't include the id in list items.
  --no-indicator                  Don't include the indicator in list items.
  -p, --page <number>             The page to view in the list paginated by
                                  a <limit> option or `nb set limit`.
  --pager                         Display output in the pager.
  --paths                         Print the full path to each item.
  -s, --sort                      Order notes by id.
  -r, --reverse                   List items in reverse order.
  --tags                          List tags in the notebook or folder.
  -t, --type <type>, --<type>     List items of <type>. <type> can be a file
                                  extension or one of the following types:
                                  archive, audio, book, bookmark, document,
                                  folder, image, note, text, video

Description:
  List notebooks and notes in the current notebook, displaying note titles
  when available. `nb ls` is a combination of `nb notebooks` and
  `nb list` in one view.

  When <id>, <filename>, <path>, or <title> are present, the listing for the
  matching note is displayed. When no match is found, titles and filenames
  are searched for any that match <query> as a case-insensitive regular
  expression.

  Options are passed through to `list`. For more information, see
  `nb help list`.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#listing--filtering

Indicators:
  ğŸ”‰  Audio
  ğŸ“–  Book
  ğŸ”–  Bookmark
  ğŸ”’  Encrypted
  ğŸ“‚  Folder
  ğŸŒ„  Image
  ğŸ“„  PDF, Word, or Open Office document
  ğŸ“¹  Video

See Also:
  nb help browse
  nb help list
  nb help pin
  nb help search
  nb help unpin

Examples:
  nb
  nb --all
  nb ls
  nb ls example.md -e 10
  nb ls --excerpt --no-id
  nb ls --reverse
  nb ls "^Example.*"
  nb ls --10
  nb ls --type document
  nb example:
  nb example: -ae
  nb example:ls

Shortcut Alias:
  nb
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#move){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="move"} `move`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Moving & Renaming](#-moving--renaming), [`copy`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#copy), [`delete`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#delete), [`edit`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#edit)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb move ([<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id> | <filename> | <title>])
          ([<notebook>:][<path>] | --reset | --to-bookmark | --to-note |
          --to-title | --to-todo) [-f | --force]

Options:
  -f, --force     Skip the confirmation prompt.
  --reset         Reset the filename to the last modified timestamp.
  --to-bookmark   Preserve the existing filename and replace the extension
                  with ".bookmark.md" to convert the note to a bookmark.
  --to-note       Preserve the existing filename and replace the bookmark's
                  ".bookmark.md" extension with ".md" to convert the bookmark
                  to a Markdown note.
  --to-title      Set the filename to the note title, lowercased with spaces
                  and disallowed filename characters replaced with underscores.
  --to-todo       Preserve the existing filename and replace the extension
                  with ".todo.md" to convert the note to a todo.

Description:
  Move or rename a note. Move the note to <path> or change the file type.
  When the file extension is omitted, the existing extension is used.
  When only a file extension is specified, only the extension will be updated.

  `nb move` and `nb rename` are aliases and can be used interchangeably.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-moving--renaming

See Also:
  nb help copy
  nb help delete
  nb help edit

Examples:
  # move "example.md" to "sample.org"
  nb move example.md sample.org

  # rename note 3 ("example.md") to "New Name.md"
  nb rename 3 "New Name"

  # rename "example.bookmark.md" to "New Name.bookmark.md"
  nb move example.bookmark.md "New Name"

  # rename note 3 ("example.md") to a bookmark named "example.bookmark.md"
  nb rename 3 --to-bookmark

  # move note 12 into "Sample Folder" in the "demo" notebook
  nb move example:12 demo:Sample\ Folder/

  # rename note 12 in the "example" notebook to "sample.md"
  nb rename example:12 "sample.md"

  # change the file extension of note 5 to .org
  nb rename 5 .org

Alias:
  nb rename

Shortcut Alias:
  nb mv
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#notebooks){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="notebooks"} `notebooks`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#notebooks}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Notebooks](#-notebooks), [`archive`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#archive), [`history`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#history), [`move`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#move), [`remote`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#remote), [`status`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#status), [`sync`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#sync), [`unarchive`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#unarchive), [`use`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#use)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb notebooks [<name> | <query>] [--ar | --archived] [--global] [--local]
               [--names] [--paths] [--unar | --unarchived]
  nb notebooks add ([<name>] [<remote-url> [<branch>... | --all]]) [--author]
                   [--email <email>] [--name <name>]
  nb notebooks (archive | open | peek | status | unarchive) [<name>]
  nb notebooks author [<name> | <path>] [--email <email>] [--name <name>]
  nb notebooks current [--path | --selected | --filename [<filename>]]
                       [--global | --local]
  nb notebooks delete <name> [-f | --force]
  nb notebooks (export <name> [<path>] | import <path>)
  nb notebooks init [<path> [<remote-url> [<branch>]]] [--author]
                    [--email <email>] [--name <name>]
  nb notebooks rename <old-name> <new-name>
  nb notebooks select <selector>
  nb notebooks show (<name> | <path> | <selector>) [--ar | --archived]
                    [--escaped | --name | --path | --filename [<filename>]]
  nb notebooks use <name>

Options:
  --all                    Add notebooks from all remote branches.
  --ar, --archived         List archived notebooks, or return archival status
                           with `show`.
  --author                 Set the notebook's commit author email and name.
  --email <email>          Set the notebook's commit author email to <email>.
  --escaped                Print the notebook name with spaces escaped.
  --filename [<filename>]  Print an available filename for the notebooks. When
                           <filename> is provided, check for an existing file
                           and provide a filename with an appended sequence
                           number for uniqueness.
  -f, --force              Skip the confirmation prompt.
  --global                 List global notebooks or the notebook set globally
                           with `use`.
  --local                  Exit with 0 if current within a local notebook,
                           otherwise exit with 1.
  --name, --names          Print the notebook name.
  --name <name>            Set the notebook's commit author name to <name>.
  --path, --paths          Print the notebook path.
  --selected               Exit with 0 if the current notebook differs from
                           the current global notebook, otherwise exit with 1.
  --unar, --unarchived     Only list unarchived notebooks.

Subcommands:
  (default)  List notebooks.
  add        Create a new global notebook. When <remote-url> is specified,
             create one ore more new global notebook by cloning selected
             or specified <branch>es from <remote-url>.
             Aliases: `nb notebooks create`, `nb notebooks new`
  archive    Set the current notebook or notebook <name> to "archived" status.
  author     Configure the commit author email and name for the notebook.
  current    Print the current notebook name or path.
  delete     Delete a notebook.
  export     Export the notebook <name> to the current directory or <path>,
             making it usable as a local notebook.
  import     Import the local notebook at <path> to make it global.
  init       Create a new local notebook. Specify a <path> or omit to
             initialize the current working directory as a local notebook.
             Specify <remote-url> to clone an existing notebook.
  open       Open the current notebook directory or notebook <name> in the
             file browser, explorer, or finder.
             Shortcut Alias: `o`
  peek       Open the current notebook directory or notebook <name> in the
             first tool found in the following list:
             `ranger` [1], `mc` [2], `vifm` [3], `joshuto` [4], `exa` [5], or `ls`.
             Shortcut Alias: `p`
  rename     Rename a notebook. Aliases: `move`, `mv`
  select     Set the current notebook from a colon-prefixed selector.
             Not persisted. Selection format: <notebook>:<identifier>
  status     Print the archival status of the current notebook or
             notebook <name>.
  show       Show and return information about a specified notebook.
  unarchive  Remove "archived" status from the current notebook or notebook <name>.
  use        Switch to a notebook.

    1. https://ranger.github.io/
    2. https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Midnight_Commander
    3. https://vifm.info/
    4. https://github.com/kamiyaa/joshuto
    5. https://github.com/ogham/exa

Description:
  Manage notebooks.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-notebooks

See Also:
  nb help archive
  nb help history
  nb help move
  nb help remote
  nb help status
  nb help sync
  nb help unarchive
  nb help use

Examples:
  nb notebooks --names
  nb notebooks add sample
  nb notebooks add example https://github.com/example/example.git
  nb nb current --path
  nb nb archive example

Shortcut Aliases:
  nb n
  nb nb
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#open){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="open"} `open`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Viewing Bookmarks](#viewing-bookmarks), [Images](#-images), [`bookmark`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#bookmark), [`browse`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#browse), [`peek`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#peek), [`show`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#show)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb open ([<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id> | <filename> | <title>])

Description:
  Open an item or notebook. When the item is a bookmark, open the bookmarked
  page in your system's primary web browser. When the item is in a text format
  or any other file type, `open` is the equivalent of `edit`. `open`
  with a notebook opens the notebook folder in the system's file browser.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#viewing-bookmarks

See also:
  nb help bookmark
  nb help browse
  nb help peek
  nb help show

Examples:
  nb open 3
  nb open example.bookmark.md
  nb 3 open
  nb example:open 12
  nb open example:12
  nb example:12 open
  nb o 3
  nb 3 o
  nb o example:12
  nb example:12 o

Shortcut Alias:
  nb o
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#peek){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="peek"} `peek`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

``` highlight
Description:

  the bookmarked page in your terminal web browser. When the note is in a text
  format or any other file type, `peek` is the equivalent of `show`. When
  used with a notebook, `peek` opens the notebook folder first tool found in
  the following list: `ranger` [1], `mc` [2], `vifm` [3], `joshuto` [4],
  `exa` [5], or `ls`.

    1. https://ranger.github.io/
    2. https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Midnight_Commander

  nb help show
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#remote){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="remote"} `remote`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Git Sync](#-git-sync), [History](#-revision-history), [`history`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#history), [`notebooks`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#notebooks), [`status`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#status), [`sync`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#sync)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb remote
  nb remote branches [<url>]
  nb remote delete <branch-name>
  nb remote remove
  nb remote rename [<branch-name>] <name>
  nb remote reset <branch-name>
  nb remote set <url> [<branch-name>]

Subcommands:
  (default)  Print the remote URL and branch for the notebook.
  branches   List branches on the current or given remote.
  delete     Delete <branch-name> from the remote.
             Caveat: only orphan branches can be deleted.
  remove     Remove the remote URL from the notebook.
             Alias: `unset`
  rename     Rename the current orphan branch or <branch-name> to <name>.
             Caveat: only orphan branches can be renamed.
  reset      Reset <branch-name> on the remote to a blank initial state.
  set        Set the remote URL and branch for the notebook.

Description:
  Configure the remote repository URL and branch for the current notebook.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-git-sync
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-revision-history

  nb help history
  nb help notebooks
  nb help status
  nb help sync

Examples:
  nb remote set https://github.com/example/example.git
  nb remote remove
  nb example-notebook:remote set https://github.com/example/example.git
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#search){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="search"} `search`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#search}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Search](#-search), [`browse`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#browse), [`list`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#list), [`ls`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#ls)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb search ([<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id> | <filename> | <title>])
            <query>... [-a | --all] [--and <query>] [--not <query>] [--or <query>]
            [-l | --list] [--path] [-t <tag1>,<tag2>... | --tag <tag1>,<tag2>...]
            [-t | --tags] [--type <type> | --<type>] [--utility <name>]

Options:
  -a, --all                     Search all unarchived notebooks.
  --and <query>                 Add a AND query.
  -l, --list                    Print the id, filename, and title listing for
                                each matching file, without the excerpt.
  --not <query>                 Add a NOT query.
  --or  <query>                 Add an OR query.
  --path                        Print the full path for each matching file.
  -t, --tag <tag1>,<tag2>...    A comma-separated list of tags.
  -t, --tags                    List all tags found in the notebook.
  --type <type>, --<type>       Search items of <type>. <type> can be a file
                                extension or one of the following types:
                                note, bookmark, document, archive, image,
                                video, audio, folder, text
  --utility <name>              The name of the search utility to search with.

Description:
  Perform a full text search.

  Multiple query arguments are treated as AND queries, returning items that
  match all queries. AND queries can also be specified with the --and <query>
  option. The --or <query> option can be used to specify an OR query,
  returning items that match at least one of the queries. --not <query>
  excludes items matching <query>.

  `nb search` is powered by Git's built-in `git grep` tool. `nb` also
  supports performing searches with alternative search tools using the
  --utility <name> option.

  Supported alternative search tools:
    1. `rga`   https://github.com/phiresky/ripgrep-all
    2. `rg`    https://github.com/BurntSushi/ripgrep
    3. `ag`    https://github.com/ggreer/the_silver_searcher
    4. `ack`   https://beyondgrep.com/
    5. `grep`  https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grep

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-search

See Also:
  nb help browse
  nb help list
  nb help ls

Examples:
  # search current notebook for "example query"
  nb search "example query"

  # search the notebook "example" for "example query"
  nb search example: "example query"

  # search all notebooks for "example query" and list matching items
  nb search "example query" --all --list

  # search for items matching "Example" AND "Demo"
  nb search "Example" "Demo"
  nb search "Example" --and "Demo"

  # search for items matching "Example" OR "Sample"
  nb search "Example|Sample"
  nb search "Example" --or "Sample"

  # search for items matching both "Example" AND "Sample", and NOT "Demo"
  nb search "Example" --and "Sample" --not "Demo"

  # search with a regular expression
  nb search "\d\d\d-\d\d\d\d"

  # search for tags
  nb search --tag tag1 -t tag2

  # search the current notebook for "example query"
  nb q "example query"

  # search all notebooks for "example query" and list matching items
  nb q -la "example query"

Shortcut Alias:
  nb q
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#settings){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="settings"} `settings`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [`set`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} & `settings`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#%EF%B8%8F-set--settings), [Variables](#-variables), [`unset`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#unset)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb set [<name> [<value>] | <number> [<value>]]
  nb settings colors [<number> | themes]
  nb settings edit
  nb settings get   (<name> | <number>)
  nb settings list  [--long]
  nb settings set   (<name> | <number>) <value>
  nb settings show  (<name> | <number>)
  nb settings unset (<name> | <number>)

Subcommands:
  (default)  Open the settings prompt, to <name> or <number>, if present.
             When <value> is also present, assign <value> to the setting.
  colors     Print a table of available colors and their xterm color numbers.
             When <number> is provided, print the number in its color.
             `settings colors themes` prints a list of installed themes.
  edit       Open the `nb` configuration file in `$EDITOR`.
  get        Print the value of a setting.
  list       List information about available settings.
  set        Assign <value> to a setting.
  show       Print the help information and current value of a setting.
  unset      Unset a setting, returning it to the default value.

Description:
  Configure `nb`. Use `nb settings set` to customize a setting and
  `nb settings unset` to restore the default for a setting.

  Use the `nb set` alias to quickly assign values to settings:

    nb set color_theme blacklight
    nb set limit 40

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#%EF%B8%8F-set--settings

See Also:
  nb help unset

Examples:
  nb settings
  nb set 5 "org"
  nb set color_primary 105
  nb set unset color_primary
  nb set color_secondary unset
  nb settings colors
  nb settings colors 105
  nb set limit 15

Alias:
  nb set
```

``` highlight
     ---------

     â€¢ Default Value: 1
```

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#header){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="header"} `header`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

``` highlight
[9]  header
     ------
     By default, `nb` and `nb ls` include a header listing available notebooks.
     Set the alignment, or hide the header with "0".

     â€¢ Supported Values:

         0  Hide Header
         1  Dynamic Alignment
              - Left justified when list is shorter than terminal width.
              - Center aligned when list is longer than terminal width.
         2  Center Aligned (default)
         3  Left Justified

     â€¢ Default Value: 1
```

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#limit){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="limit"} `limit`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Listing & Filtering](#listing--filtering)

``` highlight
[10] limit
     -----
     The maximum number of items included in the `nb` and `nb ls` lists.
     Set to `auto` to automatically limit output to the current terminal height.
     Subtract an auto limit offset for multiline prompts with `auto-<number>`.

     â€¢ Example Values:

       15
       auto
       auto-2

     â€¢ Default Value: 15
```

[â†‘Â ](#-help)

``` highlight
[11] nb_dir
     ------
     The location of the directory that contains the notebooks.

     For example, to sync all notebooks with Dropbox, create a folder at
     `~/Dropbox/Notes` and run: `nb settings set nb_dir ~/Dropbox/Notes`

     â€¢ Default Value: ~/.nb
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#shell){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="shell"} `shell`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Interactive Shell](#-interactive-shell), [`run`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#run)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb shell [<subcommand> [<options>...] | --clear-history]

Options:
  --clear-history  Clear the `nb` shell history.

Description:
  Start the `nb` interactive shell. Type "exit" to exit.

  `nb shell` recognizes all `nb` subcommands and options, providing
  a streamlined, distraction-free approach for working with `nb`.

  When <subcommand> is present, the command will run as the shell is opened.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-interactive-shell

See Also:
  nb help run

Example:
  $ nb shell
  nb> ls 3
  [3] Example

  nb> edit 3 --content "New content."
  Updated: [3] Example

  nb> notebook
  home

  nb> exit
  $
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#show){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="show"} `show`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Viewing](#viewing), [Images](#-images), [`browse`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#browse), [`open`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#open), [`peek`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#peek)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb show ([<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id> | <filename> | <title>])
          [[-a | --added] | [--authors] | [-b | --browse] | --filename | --id |
          --info-line | --path | [-p | --print] | --relative-path | [-r |
          --render] | --title | --type [<type>] | [-u | --updated]] [--no-color]
  nb show <notebook>

Options:
  -a, --added      Print the date and time when the item was added.
  --authors        List the git commit authors of an item.
  -b, --browse     Open the item with `nb browse`.
  --filename       Print the filename of the item.
  --id             Print the id number of the item.
  --info-line      Print the id, filename, and title of the item.
  --no-color       Show without syntax highlighting.
  --path           Print the full path of the item.
  -p, --print      Print to standard output / terminal.
  --relative-path  Print the item's path relative within the notebook.
  -r, --render     Use `pandoc` [1] to render the file to HTML and display
                   in the terminal web browser. If either `pandoc` or a
                   browser are unavailable, `-r` / `--render` is ignored.
  --title          Print the title of the note.
  --type [<type>]  Print the file extension or, when <type> is specified,
                   return true if the item matches <type>. <type> can be a
                   file extension or one of the following types:
                   archive, audio, bookmark, document, folder, image,
                   text, video
  -u, --updated    Print the date and time of the last recorded change.

Description:
  Show an item or notebook. Notes in text file formats can be rendered or
  printed to standard output. Non-text files are opened in your system's
  preferred app or program for that file type.

  By default, the item is opened using `less` or the program configured
  in the `$PAGER` environment variable. Use the following keys to navigate
  in `less` (see `man less` for more information):

    Key               Function
    ---               --------
    mouse scroll      Scroll up or down
    arrow up or down  Scroll one line up or down
    f                 Jump forward one window
    b                 Jump back one window
    d                 Jump down one half window
    u                 Jump up one half window
    /<query>          Search for <query>
    n                 Jump to next <query> match
    q                 Quit

  To skip the pager and print to standard output, use the `-p` / `--print`
  option.

  `-r` / `--render` automatically uses either `w3m` [2] or `links` [3].
  To specify a preferred browser, set the `$BROWSER` environment variable
  in your .bashrc, .zshrc, or equivalent, e.g.: export BROWSER="links"

  If `bat` [4], `highlight` [5], or Pygments [6] is installed, notes are
  printed with syntax highlighting.

    1. https://pandoc.org/
    2. https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/W3m
    3. https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Links_(web_browser)
    4. https://github.com/sharkdp/bat
    5. http://www.andre-simon.de/doku/highlight/en/highlight.php
    6. https://pygments.org/

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#viewing

See Also:
  nb help browse
  nb help open
  nb help peek

Examples:
  nb show 1
  nb show example.md --render
  nb show "A Document Title" --print --no-color
  nb 1 show
  nb example:show 12
  nb show example:12
  nb example:12 show
  nb s 1
  nb 1 s
  nb s example:12
  nb example:12 s

Alias:
  nb view

Shortcut Alias:
  nb s
```

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Plugins](#-plugins), [`plugins`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#plugins)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb subcommands [add <name>...] [alias <name> <alias>]
                 [describe <name> <usage>]

Subcommands:
  add       Add a new subcommand.
  alias     Create an <alias> of a given subcommand <name>, with linked help.
            Note that aliases must also be added with `subcommands add`.
  describe  Set the usage text displayed with `nb help <subcommand>`.
            This can be assigned as a heredoc, which is recommended, or
            as a string argument.

Description:
  List, add, alias, and describe subcommands. New subcommands, aliases, and
  descriptions are not persisted, so `add`, `alias`, `describe` are
  primarily for plugins.

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-plugins

See Also:
  nb help plugins
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#sync){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="sync"} `sync`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘](#-help) Â· See also: [Git Sync](#-git-sync), [History](#-revision-history), [`history`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#history), [`notebooks`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#notebooks), [`remote`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#remote), [`status`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#status)

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb sync [-a | --all]

Options:
  -a, --all   Sync all unarchived notebooks.

Description:
  Sync the current notebook with its remote.

Private Repositories and Git Credentials:
  Syncing with private repositories requires configuring git to not prompt
  for credentials.

  For repositories cloned over HTTPS, credentials can be cached with git.
  For repositories cloned over SSH, keys can be added to the ssh-agent.

  More Information:
    https://github.com/xwmx/nb#private-repositories-and-git-credentials

Sync Conflict Resolution:
  When `nb sync` encounters a conflict in a text file and can't merge
  overlapping local and remote changes, both versions are saved in the
  file, separated by git conflict markers. Use `nb edit` to remove the
  conflict markers and delete any unwanted text.

  When `nb sync` encounters a conflict in a binary file, such as an
  encrypted note or bookmark, both versions of the file are saved in the
  notebook as individual files, one with `--conflicted-copy` appended to
  the filename.

  More Information:
    https://github.com/xwmx/nb#sync-conflict-resolution

Read More:
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-git-sync
  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-revision-history

See Also:
  nb help history
  nb help notebooks
  nb help remote
  nb help status

Examples:
  nb sync
  nb sync --all
```

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb todo add [<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<filename>] <title>
              [--description <description>] [--due <date>]
              [-r (<url> | <selector>) | --related (<url> | <selector>)]
              [--tags <tag1>,<tag2>...] [--task <title>]...

                 [open | closed]

Options:
  --description <description>         Description for the todo.
  --due <date>                        Due date and / or time for the todo.
  -r, --related (<url> | <selector>)  Related URL or selector.
  --tags <tag1>,<tag2>...             Comma-separated list of tags.
  --task <title>                      Task to add to the tasklist.

Subcommands:
  (default)   List todos.
  add         Add a new todo.
              Shortcut Aliases: `nb todo a`, `nb todo +`
  do          Mark a todo or task as done.
  tasks       List tasks in todos, notebooks, folders, and other item.
  undo        Unmark a todo or task as done.

Description:
  Manage todos and tasks.

  https://github.com/xwmx/nb#-todos

  nb help do
  nb help tasks
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#backlink){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="backlink"} `backlink`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘Â ](#plugin-help)

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#install){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="install"} Install

``` highlight
nb plugins install https://github.com/xwmx/nb/blob/master/plugins/backlink.nb-plugin
```

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#help-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="help-1"} Help {#help-1}

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb backlink [--force]

Description:
  Add backlinks to notes. Crawl notes in a notebook for [[wiki-style links]]
  and append a "Backlinks" section to each linked file that lists passages
  referencing the note.

  To link to a note from within another note, surround the title of the
  target note in double square brackets:

      Example with link to [[Target Note Title]] in content.

  Depends on note-link-janitor:
    https://github.com/andymatuschak/note-link-janitor

    Requirement: every note in the notebook must have a title.
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#bump){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="bump"} `bump`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘Â ](#plugin-help)

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#install-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="install-1"} Install


##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#help-2){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="help-2"} Help {#help-2}

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb bump [<notebook>:][<folder-path>/][<id>][<filename>][<title>]

Description:
  Bump an item to the top of the list.

  `bump` updates the item's modification timestamp without editing the item
  or creating a new commit.

Examples:
  nb bump 123
  nb bump example:sample/456

Alias:
  nb touch
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#clip){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="clip"} `clip`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘Â ](#plugin-help)

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#install-2){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="install-2"} Install


##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#help-3){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="help-3"} Help {#help-3}

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb clip [<notebook>:][<id> | <filename> | <path> | <title> | <extension>]

Description:
  Save the clipboard contents and copy contents of text or markdown items to
  the clipboard.

  When called with no arguments or when no matching file is found, the text
  content on the clipboard is saved to a new file, pending a prompt.

Examples:
  # copy the content of item 123 to the clipboard
  nb clip 123

  # save the clipboard contents to a new file with a `.js` file extension
  nb clip .js

  # save the clipboard contents as a new `.cr` file in the "snippets" notebook
  nb snippets:clip .cr
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#ebook){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="ebook"} `ebook`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

[â†‘Â ](#plugin-help)

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#install-3){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="install-3"} Install

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#help-4){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="help-4"} Help {#help-4}

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb ebook new <name>
  nb ebook publish

Subcommands:
  ebook new      Create a new notebook initialized with placeholder files for
                 authoring an ebook.
  ebook publish  Generate a .epub file using the current notebook contents.

Description:
  Ebook authoring with `nb`.

  `nb ebook new` creates a notebook populated with initial placeholder files
  for creating an ebook. Edit the title page and chapters using normal `nb`
  commands, then use `nb ebook publish` to generate an epub file.

  Chapters are expected to be markdown files with sequential numeric
  filename prefixes for ordering:

    01-example.md
    02-sample.md
    03-demo.md

  Create new chapters with `nb add`:

    nb add --filename "04-chapter4.md"

  title.txt contains the book metadata in a YAML block. For more information
  about the fields for this file, visit:

    https://pandoc.org/MANUAL.html#epub-metadata

  stylesheet.css contains base styling for the generated ebook. It can be used
  as it is and can also be edited using `nb edit`.

  As with all `nb` notebooks, changes are recorded automatically in git,
  providing automatic version control for all ebook content, source, and
  metadata files.

  Generated epub files are saved in the notebook and can be previewed in the
  terminal with `nb show`. Export a generated epub file with `nb export`:

    nb export 12 .

More info:
  https://pandoc.org/epub.html
```

### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-variables){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-variables"} `$`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Variables {#-variables}

^[â†‘](#overview)\ Â·\ [`set`&`settings`](#%EF%B8%8F-set--settings),\ [`nb settings`](#settings)^

^[`$EDITOR`](#editor-1)Â Â·\ [`$NB_ACE_ENABLED`](#nb_ace_enabled)Â Â·\ [`$NB_ACE_MD_GUTTER`](#nb_ace_md_gutter)Â Â·\ [`$NB_ACE_RELATIVE_LINE_NUMBERS`](#nb_ace_relative_line_numbers)Â Â·\ [`$NB_ACE_SOFT_TABS`](#nb_ace_soft_tabs)Â Â·\ [`$NB_ACE_KEYBOARD`](#nb_ace_keyboard)Â Â·\ [`$NB_AUDIO_TOOL`](#nb_audio_tool)Â Â·\ [`$NB_AUTO_SYNC`](#nb_auto_sync)Â Â·\ [`$NB_BROWSER`](#nb_browser)Â Â·\ [`$NB_COLOR_PRIMARY`](#nb_color_primary)Â Â·\ [`$NB_COLOR_SECONDARY`](#nb_color_secondary)Â Â·\ [`$NB_COLOR_THEME`](#nb_color_theme)Â Â·\ [`$NB_DATA_TOOL`](#nb_data_tool)Â Â·\ [`$NB_DEFAULT_EXTENSION`](#nb_default_extension)Â Â·\ [`$NB_DIR`](#nb_dir-1)Â Â·\ [`$NB_DIRECTORY_TOOL`](#nb_directory_tool)Â Â·\ [`$NB_ENCRYPTION_TOOL`](#nb_encryption_tool)Â Â·\ [`$NB_FOOTER`](#nb_footer)Â Â·\ [`$NB_GUI_BROWSER`](#nb_gui_browser)Â Â·\ [`$NB_HEADER`](#nb_header)Â Â·\ [`$NB_IMAGE_TOOL`](#nb_image_tool)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_AUDIO`](#nb_indicator_audio)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_BOOKMARK`](#nb_indicator_bookmark)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_DOCUMENT`](#nb_indicator_document)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_EBOOK`](#nb_indicator_ebook)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_ENCRYPTED`](#nb_indicator_encrypted)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_FOLDER`](#nb_indicator_folder)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_IMAGE`](#nb_indicator_image)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_PINNED`](#nb_indicator_pinned)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_TODO`](#nb_indicator_todo)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_TODO_DONE`](#nb_indicator_todo_done)Â Â·\ [`$NB_INDICATOR_VIDEO`](#nb_indicator_video)Â Â·\ [`$NB_LIMIT`](#nb_limit)Â Â·\ [`$NB_MATHJAX_ENABLED`](#nb_mathjax_enabled)Â Â·\ [`$NB_PINNED_PATTERN`](#nb_pinned_pattern)Â Â·\ [`$NB_SERVER_HOST`](#nb_server_host)Â Â·\ [`$NB_SERVER_PORT`](#nb_server_port)Â Â·\ [`$NB_SYNTAX_THEME`](#nb_syntax_theme)Â Â·\ [`$NB_USER_AGENT`](#nb_user_agent)Â Â·\ [`$NBRC_PATH`](#nbrc_path)^

[Â â†‘Â ](#overview)

[Settings](#%EF%B8%8F-set--settings) are set in the `~/.nbrc`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} configuration file using environment variables. Settings can be set through `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} using [`set`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} & `settings`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#%EF%B8%8F-set--settings) or by assigning a value to the variable directly in the `~/.nbrc`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} file, which can be opened in your `$EDITOR`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} with [`nb settings edit`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#settings).

Example assignment:

``` highlight
export NB_INDICATOR_PINNED="ğŸ”®"
```

^[â†‘](#-variables)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#editor-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="editor-1"} `$EDITOR`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

``` highlight
The terminal editor command for editing items.
```

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#nb_limit){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="nb_limit"} `$NB_LIMIT`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

``` highlight
Default: '15'

Set to a positive number to limit the output of `nb` and `nls` to that value.
Set to "auto" to automatically limit output to the current terminal height.
Subtract an auto limit offset for multiline prompts with `auto-<number>`.

Supported Values:
  - <number>
  - auto-<number>
  - auto-<number>

Example Values:
  - 15
  - auto
  - auto-2
```

## [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#specifications){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="specifications"} Specifications

[Bookmark File Format](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)Â Â· [Todo File Format](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)Â Â· [Notebook Specification](#nb-notebook-specification)

[Â â†‘Â ](#-help)

### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format"} `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Markdown Bookmark File Format

^[â†‘](#specifications)\ Â·\ [Bookmarks](#-bookmarks),\ [`nb bookmark`](#bookmark)^

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#extension){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="extension"} Extension

`.bookmark.md`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#description){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="description"} Description

`nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} bookmarks are Markdown documents created using a combination of user input and data from the bookmarked page. The `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} bookmark format is intended to be readable, editable, convertible, renderable, and clearly organized for greatest accessibility.

Bookmarks are identified by a `.bookmark.md`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} file extension. The bookmark URL is the first URL in the file within `<`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} and `>`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} characters. To create a minimally valid bookmark file with [`nb add`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#add):

``` highlight
nb add example.bookmark.md --content "<https://example.com>"
```

This creates a file with the name `example.bookmark.md`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} containing:

``` highlight
<https://example.com>
```

In a full bookmark, information is separated into sections, with each bookmark section indicated by a Markdown `h2`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} heading.

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#example-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="example-1"} Example

```` highlight
# Example Title (example.com)

<https://example.com>

## Description

Example description.

## Quote

> Example quote line one.
>
> Example quote line two.

## Comment

Example comment.

## Related

- <https://example.net>
- <https://example.org>
- [[example:123]]

## Tags

#tag1 #tag2

## Content

Example Title
=============

This domain is for use in illustrative examples in documents. You may
use this domain in literature without prior coordination or asking for
permission.

[More information\...](https://www.iana.org/domains/example)

## Source

```html
<!doctype html>
<html>
  <head>
    <title>Example Title</title>
    <meta name="description" content="Example description." />
  </head>

  <body>
    <h1>Example Title</h1>
    <p>
      This domain is for use in illustrative examples in documents. You may
      use this domain in literature without prior coordination or asking for
      permission.
    </p>
    <p>
      <a href="https://www.iana.org/domains/example">More information...</a>
    </p>
  </body>
</html>
```
````

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#elements){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="elements"} Elements

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#title){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="title"} Title

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A [Markdown atx-style `h1`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} heading](https://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/syntax#header) containing the content of the bookmarked page's HTML `<title>`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} or [`og:title`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](https://ogp.me/) tag, if present, followed by the domain within parentheses.

###### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#examples-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="examples-1"} Examples

``` highlight
# Example Title (example.com)
```

``` highlight
# (example.com)
```

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#url){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="url"} URL

`Required`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

The URL of the bookmarked resource, with surrounding angle brackets (`<`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}, `>`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}).

This is the only required element.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-description){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-description"} `## Description`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-description}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A text element containing the content of the bookmarked page's meta description or [`og:description`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](https://ogp.me/) tag, if present.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-quote){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-quote"} `## Quote`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-quote}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A markdown quote block containing a user-specified excerpt from the bookmarked resource.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-comment){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-comment"} `## Comment`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-comment}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A text element containing a comment written by the user.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-related){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-related"} `## Related`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-related}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A Markdown list of angle bracketed (`<`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}, `>`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}) URLs and [\[\[wiki-style links\]\]](#-linking) that are related to the bookmarked resource.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-tags){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-tags"} `## Tags`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-tags}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A list of [#tags](#-tagging) represented as `#hashtags`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} separated by individual spaces.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-content){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-content"} `## Content`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-content}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

The full content of the bookmarked page, converted to Markdown.

The `## Content`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} section makes the page content available locally for full-text search and viewing of page content. The source HTML is converted to inline Markdown to reduce the amount of markup, make it more readable, and make page content easily viewable in the terminal as markdown and streamlined HTML in web browsers.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-source){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-source"} `## Source`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-source}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A fenced code block with `html`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} language identifier containing the source HTML from the bookmarked page.

`nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} does not save the page source by default. `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} uses this section to save the source HTML page content when `pandoc`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} is not available to convert it to Markdown.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-bookmark-file-format)^

### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="nb-markdown-todo-file-format"} `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Markdown Todo File Format

^[â†‘](#specifications)\ Â·\ [Todos](#-todos),\ [`nb todo`](#todo)^

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#extension-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="extension-1"} Extension

`.todo.md`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#description-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="description-1"} Description {#description-1}

`nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} todos are Markdown documents identified by a `.todo.md`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} file extension. Todos contain a Markdown `h1`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} heading starting with a Markdown checkbox (`[ ]`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} / `[x]`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}) indicating the todo completion state, followed by the todo title.

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#example-2){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="example-2"} Example

``` highlight
# [x] Example todo title.

## Due

2100-01-01

## Description

Example description.

## Tasks

- [ ] One
- [x] Two
- [ ] Three

## Related

- [[example:123]]
- <https://example.org>

## Tags

#tag1 #tag2
```

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#elements-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="elements-1"} Elements

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#title-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="title-1"} Title

`Required`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A [Markdown atx-style `h1`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} heading](https://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/syntax#header) containing a Markdown checkbox followed by the todo title. An `x`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} within the checkbox (`[ ]`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}) indicates that the todo is done.

###### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#examples-2){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="examples-2"} Examples

``` highlight
# [ ] Example undone / open todo title.
```

``` highlight
# [x] Example done / closed todo title.
```

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-due){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-due"} `## Due`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-due}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A text element containing a value referencing a due date and / or time for the todo.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-description-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-description-1"} `## Description`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-description-1}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A text element containing a description for the todo.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-tasks){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-tasks"} `## Tasks`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-tasks}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A markdown tasklist containing sub-tasks for the todo.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-related-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-related-1"} `## Related`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-related-1}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A Markdown list of angle bracketed (`<`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}, `>`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}) URLs and [\[\[wiki-style links\]\]](#-linking) that are related to the todo.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)^

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#-tags-1){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="-tags-1"} `## Tags`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} {#-tags-1}

`Optional`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

A list of [#tags](#-tagging) represented as `#hashtags`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} separated by individual spaces.

^[â†‘](#nb-markdown-todo-file-format)^

### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#nb-notebook-specification){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="nb-notebook-specification"} `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Notebook Specification

^[â†‘](#specifications)\ Â·\ [Notebooks](#-notebooks),\ [`nb notebooks`](#notebooks)^

An `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} notebook is a directory that contains a valid `.git`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} directory, indicating that it has been initialized as a git repository, and a `.index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} file in the root directory.

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#index-files){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="index-files"} `.index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Files

A notebook folder index is a text file named `.index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} in any folder within the notebook directory. `.index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} contains a list of visible filenames within the folder, one per line, and the line number of each filename represents the id. `.index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} files are included in the git repository so ids are preserved across systems.

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#operations){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="operations"} Operations

`add`
:   Append a new line containing the filename to `.index`.

`update`
:   Overwrite the existing filename in `.index` with the new filename.

`delete`
:   Delete the filename, preserving the newline, leaving the line blank.

`reconcile`
:   Remove duplicate lines, preserving existing blank lines, `add` entries for new files, and `delete` entries for deleted files.

`rebuild`
:   Delete and rebuild `.index`, listing files by most recently modified, reversed.

##### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#index-subcommand){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="index-subcommand"} `index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Subcommand

`nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} manages the `.index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} of each folder within a notebook using an internal `index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} subcommand.

###### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#nb-help-index){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="nb-help-index"} `nb help index`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}

``` highlight
Usage:
  nb index add <filename>
  nb index delete <filename>
  nb index get_basename <id>
  nb index get_id <filename>
  nb index get_max_id
  nb index rebuild [--ancestors]
  nb index reconcile [--ancestors] [--commit]
  nb index show
  nb index update <existing-filename> <new-filename>
  nb index verify
  nb index <subcommand> <options>... [<folder-path>]

Options:
  --ancestors   Perform the action on all folders within the notebook that
                are ancestors of the current folder.
  --commit      Commit changes to git.

Subcommands:
  add           Add <filename> to the index.
  delete        Delete <filename> from the index.
  get_basename  Print the filename / basename at the specified <id>.
  get_id        Get the id for <filename>.
  get_max_id    Get the maximum id for the folder.
  rebuild       Rebuild the index, listing files by last modified, reversed.
                Some ids will change. Prefer `nb index reconcile`.
  reconcile     Remove duplicates and update index for added and deleted files.
  show          Print the index.
  update        Overwrite the <existing-filename> entry with <new-filename>.
  verify        Verify that the index matches the folder contents.

Description:
  Manage the index for the current folder or the folder at <folder-path>,
  which can be passed as the final argument to any `index` subcommand.

  `index` is used internally by `nb` and using it manually will
  probably corrupt the index. If something goes wrong with an index,
  fix it with `nb index reconcile`.

  An index is a text file named '.index' in any folder within a notebook.
  .index contains a list of filenames and the line number of each filename
  represents the id. .index files are included in the git repository so
  ids are preserved across systems.
```

^[â†‘](#nb-notebook-specification)^

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#pindex-files){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="pindex-files"} `.pindex`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} Files

Any folder may contain an optional plain text file named `.pindex`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} containing a list of basenames from that folder, one per line, that should be treated as [pinned](#-pinning), meaning they appear first in some list operations, including `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} and [`nb ls`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#ls). Entries are added to a `.pindex`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} file with [`nb pin`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#pin) and removed with [`nb unpin`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}](#unpin).

^[â†‘](#nb-notebook-specification)^

#### [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#archived-notebooks){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="archived-notebooks"} Archived Notebooks

A notebook is considered [archived](#archiving-notebooks) when it contains a file named `.archived`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} at the root level of the notebook directory.

^[â†‘](#nb-notebook-specification)^

## [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIHhsaW5rOmhyZWY9IiNzdmctbGluayIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)](#tests){.anchor-heading aria-labelledby="tests"} Tests

With more than 2,000 tests spanning tens of thousands of lines, `nb`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} is really mostly a [test suite](https://github.com/xwmx/nb/tree/master/test). Tests run continuously [via GitHub Actions](https://github.com/xwmx/nb/actions) on recent versions of both Ubuntu and macOS to account for differences between BSD and GNU tools and Bash versions. To run the tests locally, install [Bats](https://github.com/bats-core/bats-core) and the [recommended dependencies](#optional), then run `bats test`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} within the project root directory. Run groups of tests with globbing, e.g., `bats test/browse*`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge} and `bats test/folders*`{.language-plaintext .highlighter-rouge}.
